      By doing a series of specific 
      muscle areas and then a number of muscles <br>
      in the same line of your leg, arm, torso, etc, <br>

&nbsp;in the same areas by then lengthening the shortened 'fascia' part of your 
      muscles.<br>

 </font>

      <font face="Verdana">

      <font size="4">3. HOW DOES MY STRETCHING ACTUALLY WORK<br>
      WHY DOES IT GIVE BETTER RESULTS</font><br>
      <br>
      </font>

      <font color="#0000FF" face="Arial">

      This system is more thorough than many others to improve the three necessary parts:<br>
      Fascial lengthening --- Interconnected muscle groups --- Structural 
      realignment<br>
      And you can add to its effectiveness with your additional stretches<br>
      </font>

      <font color="#333333" face="Arial" size="2">

      (But it is usually insufficient to try to incorporate these individual 
      stretches into <br>
      your own routine that has not been a successful improvement method for you 
      already.)<br>
      </font>

      <font color="#CC3300">

      <font face="Arial">

      Just keep in mind these three necessary elements.</font><font face="Verdana"><br>
      </font>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial">

      <font size="5"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">More thorough fascial fiber spreading in more 
      areas<br>
      of the muscle, muscle groups, &amp; whole body.</font></font><font size="5" face="Verdana"><br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial">

      In this Structural Integration method,<br>
      what I have you do is put your body in certain positions <br>
      &amp; keep a gentle but firm pull in a long length of muscles.<br>
      Then you focus on each few inches of the longer length<br>
      to encourage the collagen fibers of the fascia in that section of the 
      muscles<br>
&nbsp;to spread one from the other, back out to their proper distances.<br>
      <br>
      <font color="#0000FF">We also get more of the muscle areas than most other stretching gets.<br>
      </font>For example, after doing say, a long stretch down a body part, <br>
      we then turn the foot, leg, arm or torso to get a couple other angles for 
      other lines<br>
      of section by section stretches moving up the line.&nbsp; <br>
      For example, we stretch the back of the legs<br>
&nbsp;in three lines, the adductors also in three lines, <br>
      and adjust the foot and leg position to get both the lower leg as well as 
      thighs longer.&nbsp; <br>
      We angle the quad stretches to lengthen the pelvic area as well as the 
      middle thighs. <br>
      The same in the torso, <br>
      besides detailed methods of stretching the front and back center lines,
      <br>
      we also do the angles of the front and back and the sides, <br>
      including on the outside, in the rib cage, and along the spine.<br>
      <font size="2"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">This multi-line method as well as the section by section of each 
      line method,<br>
      gets noticeably more length than just, for instance a stretch only down 
      the middle<br>
      </font>&nbsp;of the back of the legs.&nbsp; And in addition, lengthening one side angle<br>
&nbsp;of the same muscles enables another stretch down the middle line<br>
      to go further &amp; easier. <br>
      <font size="2"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">We also do twisting stretches to open the leg 
      and arm muscles, <br>
      separating one muscle bundle from another as there are a lot in say, the 
      thigh or arms.<br>
      </font>&nbsp; That way, the leg or arm is looser that just from the 
      lengthening stretch,<br>
      and the areas it connects to get looser as well, because the pulls <br>
      on the bones of the pelvis, for instance, the bone that also connects <br>
      to the belly and back, will then be less pulling on that bone.&nbsp; <br>
      And that bone is then less pulling and tightening on the abdominal &amp; back 
      muscles.<br>
      Also, the next lengthwise stretching of the opened thigh area goes 
      further. <br>
      The twisting releasing, which opens up more of the bone, joint and muscle<br>
&nbsp;range of motion, increases agility.<br>
      <font size="2"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">There's also a way to rotate the torso in a 
      sequence to get all the areas<br>
      &nbsp;to lengthen more, and a way to open the ribs and abdomen in 
      front,<br>
      as well as stretch the spine in back more precisely &amp; thoroughly than most 
      people do<br>
      in yoga spinal twist positions.<br>
      </font>You learn to guide subtle body movements to pull at specific areas<br>
      one after the other.&nbsp; This spreads the collagen fibers back out and 
      the areas <br>
      you have done this in will be longer and stay longer.<br>
      <font size="6">
      <br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">Why we do multiple areas and multiple lines.</font><font size="6"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">This is different from the isolated 
      stretching methods used by others<br>
      because we are lengthening the fascia bodysuit that everyone has.<span style="background-color: #FFFFCC"><br>
      </span></font>Our fascial shape, including length, is made of thousands of tiny collagen 
      fibers <br>
      throughout a gelatinous fluid that surrounds all the muscle fibers <br>
      &amp; wraps up the whole muscle.&nbsp; <br>
      It is this fibrous fascia filler &amp; wrappings that become the tendons that 
      connect<br>
      the muscle belly to the bones across the joints.&nbsp; <br>
      And with activity, including athletics, and also tension, collagen fibers 
      bunch up<br>
      closer together through the whole muscle and in many muscles, <br>
      more &amp; more&nbsp; When you get longer from Bodywork &amp; stretching, it is 
      because <br>
      you are spreading the collagen fibers back out from their bunched up 
      locations.<br>
      <font size="4"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">So to both make the muscle fiber and nerve tightness 'let go' and 
      to then <br>
      lengthen back out the distance between the many collagen fibers through 
      the whole muscle, <br>
      we are relengthening the many areas of each muscle,<br>
&nbsp;and the groups of muscles that interconnect with one 
      another.&nbsp; <br>
      </font>If you only lengthen the calf or the thigh, or in one line down the middle<br>
      of the back of the leg, you are only getting some of the distances to 
      relengthen<br>
&nbsp;while the other areas of the muscle are just as short as before.<br>
      <font size="4">

      <br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">In addition, if you only try to lengthen the one muscle in a line, <br>
      then the shortened other muscles in the next lines, are still pulling the 
      area tight.&nbsp; <br>
      </font>This is because fascia is like&nbsp; a big body suit all over the body,
      <br>
      and tightness anywhere makes its pull felt in all other areas. <br>
      It is also because the tightness of nearby muscles pulls with their 
      tendons<br>
      on the bones that this muscle is connected to, and that makes the same 
      joints<br>
      still tight and keeps a tight muscular pull throughout the whole multi 
      muscle length.<br>
      <br>
      <font color="#0000FF">Here is an example of my method in this regard. <br>
      </font>There is one kind of back of leg stretching standing,<br>
      and one lying down, that are unique groupings of areas., <br>
      and I add a modified, one legged yoga position (to get more length out of 
      it<br>
&nbsp;in the standing leg),&nbsp; and some other yoga and Physical Therapy 
      stretches<br>
      that again focus on the section by section collagen fiber spreading back 
      out apart. <br>
      <font size="2"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">I significantly improve the calf stretch type of position<br>
      </font>Not only do we do an 
      extra front to back<br>
&nbsp;pushing of the calf as we are doing the lengthwise pulling,<br>
      we also do the same technique for the ankle-heel, Achilles tendon, <br>
      behind the knee, and lower and upper thigh, as well as in the belly of the 
      calf. <br>
      In addition, we do the foot and leg turning at different angles to get 
      more of this deeper modified calf stretch (leg stretch) <br>
      <font size="2"><br>
      <br>
      </font>I have people do stretches in an order according to how tight they 
      are and<br>
      in which sequence, --&nbsp; we find by doing, will give way better.</font><font color="#666666" face="Arial" size="2"><br>
      </font><font color="#666666" face="Arial" size="4"><br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial">

      <font color="#0000FF">It is the unique positionings of the body, <br>
      the focus of your attention inside the muscles you want to lengthen, <br>
      and the longer lines of interconnected muscle groups that<br>
      enables this stretching to go further and easier.<br>
      Plus, there is a repeated set of stretches that keeps lengthening legs &amp; 
      back<br>
      as we add additional areas of stretching.<br>
      <font size="4"><br>
      </font>By understanding the alignment &amp; misalignment of the legs
      <br>
      to torso to head and neck, we can lengthen multiple areas of the whole 
      body</font><br>
      <font color="#0000FF">&nbsp;so the zig zagging of the structure front to back and side to side gets 
      less and less</font>.<br>
      It is this tilt one way and tilt the other way that keeps the body tight 
      as one part pulls back on the others, and vice versa.&nbsp; This is to try 
      to keep you upright against <br>
      the downward pull of gravity.&nbsp; But that gravity is only pulling you 
      down<br>
      because the parts of the body are tilted to it.<br>
      </font>

      <font color="#008080" face="Arial" size="4">

      <br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial">

      <font color="#0000FF">And importantly, you should know that the fascia grows<br>
      into the positions the muscles, which
      keeps holding that shape,<br>
&nbsp;as well as the tightness is repeatedly<br>
      bunching up the collagen fibers.</font><br>
      So if you can't stand upright easier and straighter after stretching<br>
      or Bodywork, then your body parts will tilt back to the compensating other 
      side,<br>
&nbsp; Even if you had loosened the legs, for instance, or the back, <br>
      then the body will be forced to retighten in the shape it did before,<br>
      just to compensate again for the parts that were not lengthened.<br>
      <font size="5">
      <br>
      </font>
      <font color="#0000FF">Spreading apart the positions of many collagen 
      fibers,<br>
      Lengthwise and across the muscles,<br>
      coupled with the arrangement of the stretches &amp; what each stretch's
      <br>
      purpose is&nbsp; in the 
      structural shape, <br>
      makes this system effective.<br>
      </font>
      <font size="2"><font color="#CC3300">Longer On-Site Article</font>&nbsp;&nbsp;
      <a href="Free_Booklets_Athletic_Enhancement_Intro.htm">Improving Athletic 
      &amp; Physical Performance with this Approach</a></font><font color="#0000FF"><br>
      </font>
      </font>

      <font size="5" color="#0000FF" face="Arial">
      <br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial"><font color="#0000FF">As I mentioned above, this creates <br>
      Significantly More Muscle Length 'Between' the 
      Joints,' <br>
      as well as at 
      the joints, that you normally 'think' is looseness.</font><br>
      So this longer&nbsp;&nbsp; Belly-of-the-Muscle&nbsp;&nbsp; LENGTH&nbsp; 
      ---&nbsp; frees joints to go further.<br>
      <font size="5"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">This</font></font><font face="Arial" color="#0000FF"> increases flexibility at the joint ,&amp; even in the way the muscles 
      themselves move.<br>
      individually and in coordinated groups.<br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial">The muscle-joint movements move together: <br>
      the bellies of the muscles lengthen and rotate along with the joints 
      themselves.<br>
&nbsp; So there is greater range of motion that is also more integrated one 
      muscle to another.<br>
      And the whole body functions more as the properly functioning system<br>
      it is designed to be --- once a lot of the shortened fascia is 
      re-lengthened.<br>
      <font size="5"><br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">This is also what fixes structural misalignment 
      ,caused by short muscle fascia,<br>
      including the structural misalignment that creates tightening the back</font><br>
      which is caused by pulling
      from other shortened body areas, especially legs.<br>
      This is
      THE MAJOR CAUSE of developing back problems.<br>
      <font size="2"><font color="#CC3300">E-book Overview &amp; Excerpt Page </font>&nbsp;&nbsp;
      <a href="Backfixbook_Menu.htm">Understanding &amp; Fixing the Underlying Cause 
      of Back Pain</a></font></font><font face="Arial" color="#800000"><font size="2"><br>
      </font>
      <font size="5">
      <br>

      </font>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#0000FF">Lengthening the Fascia of the Bellies 
      of the Muscles increases the muscle power <br>
      because the muscle fibers can then move
      a longer distance<br>
&nbsp;&amp; more of them in the muscle groups are "organized with each 
      other."<br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#333333">Lengthening the muscle belly also removes spasm pains<br>
      &amp; the chance of pulling a muscle or tendon.<br>

      </font>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial" size="4">The Typical Problem<br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#0000FF">People who have had Muscle Tightness &amp; 
      Pain&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>
      And have been Stretching, Getting Massage, Chiropractic, etc<br>
      &amp; it doesn't help much or it doesn't last<br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial">Then they are not lengthening 
      the fascia - systemically<br>
&nbsp;- 
      &amp; not in the body's front or legs.</font><font size="2" face="Arial"><br>
            <br>
      </font>

            <font size="4" face="Arial">What's needed is<br>
            </font><font face="Arial" color="#333333">You need to spread fascia all over the body, not just locally, <br>
      to re-lengthen the "interconnected muscles"<br>
&nbsp;&amp; your top-bottom &amp; left-right 
            "zig 
      zags"</font><font size="2" color="#333333" face="Arial"><br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#333333">THEN people get noticeable, fast,&nbsp; increasing 
      &amp; lasting improvements.<br>

      </font>

      <font size="5" face="Arial" color="#990033">
      <br>
      </font>

      <font size="4" face="Arial">My Effective Solution<br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#0000FF">The KEY is to spread out the 
      accumulated shortness, or bunch-up,<br>
            of the collagen fibers
      in the fascia parts of the muscles, <br>
            &amp; the way to do this well is to lengthen
            small sections at a time, <br>
            going methodically along long lines of interconnected muscles.&nbsp;<br>
            My exercises teach this.<br>

      </font>

      <font face="Arial" color="#333333">Easy to do, not straining, yet powerful good effects.<br>

      </font>

      <font size="5" face="Arial" color="#008000"><br>
      </font>

      <font color="#0000FF" face="Arial">This "method" of "fascia fiber spreading"<br>
            &nbsp;increases people's other stretches' effectiveness as well.<br>
            </font><font color="#333333" face="Arial">So instead of just isolated muscle stretches, we do section by section<br>
            spreading apart of the collagen fiber bunch-up people have had for 
      years.
      </font>

      <font size="2" color="#333333" face="Arial"><br>
            <br>
      My Method automatically teaches you about your body's misalignments &amp; how to fix them, <br>
      </font>

      <font size="2" face="Arial">Including the Cause of 
      Lower Back Pain.<br>
      </font>

      <font size="5" face="Arial" color="#008000"><br>
      </font>

      <font face="Arial">
            <font color="#333333">All our muscles and bones are interconnected<br>
            &amp; tightness even in a distant area, pulls on many other places.<br>
            So as more of the Body is relengthened, all the areas get  freer<br>
            &amp; can stretch even longer themselves.<br>
      </font><font color="#0000FF">You discover this "happy fact" with my phone coaching,<br>
            &amp; when you do the DVDs at home.<br>
      </font>
            <font size="5" color="#333333"><br>
            </font>
            <font size="4">Low Back Problems<br>
            </font><font size="2">
            <br>
            </font>These are almost always caused by 
            accumulated<br>
            shortness of the fascia in the legs and abdomen,<br>
            &amp; your whole body gets pulled forward in the legs <br>
            &amp; has to lean backward in the back, <br>
            with your internal muscles getting strained and pulling<br>
            your back vertebrae too close together.<br>
            <font size="2" color="#800000"><br>
            </font>
            <font color="#333333">In order to keep you upright and not 
            falling forward, <br>
            the back of the legs up to the back of the head gets really tight,
            <br>
            and your hips and knees get pushed too far forward <br>
            &amp; get un-natural strain put on them.<br>
            <font size="2"><br>
            </font>
            </font><font color="#0000FF">It is a classic case of overall body misalignment<br>
            from accumulated shortened fascia -<br>

      same time you help BACK pain, you also help HIP problems.&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>
      <br>

      Here's the re-lengthening concept<br>
      :&nbsp; <br>
      If you make your LEGS longer on 
      the insides (medial), &amp; front, &amp; make the front of your torso longer &amp; 
      more uplifted, as well as lengthen some of the tightness you created in 
      the back of the legs, then you can get the torso to sit over the legs, 
      instead of arching backward in the low back and maybe bent over in the 
      upper back, chest and neck.&nbsp; <br>
      <br>
      When you have to arch backward, you 
      simultaneously have to push your hips forward &amp; that makes tightness &amp; 
      misalignment in the hip joints, too, plus even more tightness in the 
      thighs and legs, including the hamstrings.<br>
      <br>
      Lengthening the front &amp; front of legs is key to loosening backs better.<br>

            <br>

      <b>

      <font face="Verdana" size="4" color="#CC3300">

      <br>

      </font>

      <font face="Verdana" size="2" color="#CC3300">

      <img border="0" src="j0295252.gif" width="55" height="80" align="left"></font><font face="Verdana">A 
      NEW Stretching &amp; Hands-on Approach<span style="background-color: #FFFF00"><br>

      </span>Why it works better, &amp;<br>

      How it can make your other stretching<br>

      work better, too.</font><font face="Verdana" size="2">&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>

                  </b>

            </p><p align="left">

      <b>

                  <font color="#006600" face="Verdana">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
      A Key reason My Methods seem to work when what people have already tried 
      didn't work as well, is because as a Structural Integration Bodyworker, 
      I've been trained to know which deep &amp; interconnected muscles need to be 
      lengthened.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; And then, &nbsp;as a college degreed engineer, I 
      teach people a specific body structure "engineering way" to do both 
      hands-on &amp; stretching movements, to lengthen all those local &amp; 
      interconnected muscles in their "fascia" parts.&nbsp; <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; It's an educational information &amp; a how-to-do-it 
      for-what-results instructional approach, rather than just a "going to a 
      class with everybody else, following along, approach."<br>

      &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font color="#CC3300" face="Verdana"> Once your tightness is 
      much looser and longer, you will be able to do, yoga classes, athletics 
      and so forth more, and enjoy it better.&nbsp; AND, you can make these 
      other activities more effective for your stretching by using these 
      interconnected-muscle, fascial spreading "methods" from my system.</font><font color="#0000FF" face="Verdana"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font>

                  <font face="Verdana">&nbsp; &nbsp;What about Pilates' lengthening?&nbsp; 
      Pilates helps a lot, but I always check people &amp; see they can be "helped" 
      by both increased lengthening in the bellies of the muscles &amp; by creating 
      a better structural alignment.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In Pilates, too, the 
      instruction is "Position like this," and "Stretch it."&nbsp; <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; But no one is telling you, 
      bring your mind's attention here, and adjust your pull with this other 
      part of the body, as well as inside the part you are stretching, so you 
      get right there, and then adjust a little further this way, and then that 
      way, to make the other parts of these muscles lengthen more, &amp; now go on 
      to the next area of muscles inch by inch in your full length of the 
      stretch.&nbsp; What do you feel?&nbsp; Test it out like this?&nbsp; If it 
      isn't going fully, go back to here.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; And now go back up 
      through the areas and pull in the opposite sequence.&nbsp; In fact, go to 
      the opposite side of the body, and instead of trying to bend and stretch 
      this new side, while contracting the first, let's try to lengthen all the 
      sides together.&nbsp; And so forth.<br>

      </font>

                  <font color="#CC3300" face="Verdana"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 

      <span style="background-color: #FFFF99">So in my method, we use a special 
      "positioning," based on structural architecture &amp; we emphasize a unique 
      mind-into-body,&nbsp;very meticulous, section by section re-lengthening&nbsp; 
      of the fascia in the bellies of the muscles,</span><span style="background-color: #FFFFCC"> 
      for the whole body sheath &amp; in-between organs.&nbsp; </span> <span style="background-color: #FFFF99">
      We pull the collagen fibers of the fascia into a longer distance.&nbsp; We 
      also do a unique separating of the bellies of each muscle from their 
      gluing onto the bellies of other muscles next to them.&nbsp;</span><br>

      &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font color="#008000" face="Verdana">&nbsp;&nbsp; In this 
      way, people always get much longer "length" sooner, &amp; that increases 
      flexibility, and strength, plus balance and power.&nbsp; It even increases 
      endurance and reduces recovery time.&nbsp; </font>

                  <font color="#006600" face="Verdana"><br>

      </font>

                  <font face="Verdana"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Olympic Level athletes 
      said that after my hands-on, they could run faster &amp; be more relaxed at 
      the same time, as well as being more relaxed, taller &amp; straighter just 
      walking around the house.&nbsp; Seniors &amp; Business people got immediate, 
      deep stress removal &amp; felt deeper ongoing relaxation, stress "immunity" &amp; 
      had better sleep.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; A very stressed 16 year 
      old said even just the first stretches on the DVD always calm her down 
      right away.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; And a number of people 
      have said that even these gentle stretches are ALSO a very good workout.<br>

      </font><font color="#CC3300" face="Verdana"><br>

      &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font color="#333333" face="Verdana">

      </font>

                  <span style="background-color: #FFFF99">

                  <font color="#333333" face="Verdana">So this method is not to 
      replace your yoga and pilates, not even your massages, but to complement 
      them, that is, to make all your stretching work better by making use of 
      how your muscles are constructed; and very significantly, to show YOU, 
      with your own body experience how to make them more effective right when 
      you do them.</font></span><font color="#0000FF" face="Verdana"><br>

      "Structural Integration - Fascia Re-lengthening."&nbsp; It restores the 
      length of the fascia soft connective<br>

      tissue in your muscles, which removes a lot of stress created tension, as 
      well as athletically&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; created tightness &amp; seniors' strain 
      to get around. <font color="#CC3300"> <br>

      bellies of your muscles&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; longer again, so that the 
      joints feel looser &amp; you gain power, strength &amp; agility at the same time.<br>

            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; It also lengthens groups of muscles that 
      are supposed to work together, but we do the stretching by lengthening 
      each little area after another.<font color="#CC3300"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

      seniors into their 80's &amp; people with significant muscle tightness &amp; 
      injury.<br>

      pulling the collagen fibers of the fascia through the fluid isn't focused 
      on.&nbsp;

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Scar tissue can be

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Structural

            <font size="4" color="#009933">Stress, Tension, Emotional Release</font></b></font><b><i><font face="Arial" color="#999999"><font size="4"><br>

            </font>

            <font size="1"><br>

            </font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></i>

            </b><font face="Arial"><b>

            <font color="#999999">&nbsp;</font><font color="#666666">&nbsp;Structural 
            Integration Bodywork is very effective for stress removal and helps 
            tight heads</font></b><font color="#666666">.

            <b>Loosening the many bones and muscles of the head increases 
            comfort and relaxation in the entire body.</b>&nbsp; </font>The many 
            pieces of the head should move, as we breathe and when we express 
            ourselves.&nbsp; But they get very tight, especially during stress.&nbsp; 
            That adversely affects the back and neck, the nervous system, the 
            ability to breathe deeply, all the internal organs, our emotional 
            capacity, and<font color="#666666"><b>

            

            </b></font>our abilities to think clearly and process large amounts 
            of information.<font color="#666666"><b><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; In my own 
            treatments for stress, I first do a lot on the head, neck, shoulders 
            and back which makes a big improvement right away.&nbsp; This also 
            removes a lot of head trauma.&nbsp; </b>In the standard 10-step 
            Structural Integration recipe, the head would not get done much, if 
            at all, until the 7th session.<b><br>

            <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Stress and back 
            pain are related.&nbsp; Having back pain, in itself, can make us 
            feel stressed.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; But we're also more 
            susceptible to the effects of stress when we're already tightened up 
            from the misaligned shape of the body.&nbsp; </b></font>

            This shape, with a big arch in the lower back, often causes back 
            pain, especially lower back pain and/or sciatica.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            <b><font color="#666666"><br>

            &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We're not very "stress immune" because of this.&nbsp; 
            The entire back of the body, including the head, neck and legs, is 
            being held tight. </font></b> <font color="#666666"><b>&nbsp;So the body 
            is already in a stressed and tense condition.&nbsp; And added 
            tightness due to the next stress just tightens it up more.</b></font><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Just a 
            little bit more tightness from the emotional reaction can bring on 
            the back pain or make it worse.&nbsp; Also, emotional tension in the 
            gut tightens the muscles connected to the vertebrae in the lower 
            back.&nbsp; Some people may get immediate lower back pain or 
            sciatica whenever this happens.<b><font color="#666666"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This 
            structural misalignment also creates a stressful behavior, one in 
            which we "have to keep going."&nbsp; We're pulled down in front and 
            we're constantly arching the lower back to pull ourselves up.&nbsp; 
            The body posture says, "I have to keep straining, even just in 
            everyday life."<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></b>

            After this shape has been corrected and the body was more balanced 
            and centered, a number of people have been able to "let down" from 
            intense work and do more things for themselves.<b><font color="#666666"><br>

            <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
            Structural Integration Bodywork is purposely designed to correct 
            this misalignment and remove the chronic tension.</font></b><font color="#666666"><b><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Working the whole 
            body, months and years of accumulated stress are removed</b></font><b><font color="#808080">

            </font><font color="#666666">at the same time that tightness all 
            over the body is re-lengthened and the shape is more straightened 
            out. </font></b>&nbsp;<font color="#666666"><b>Built-up emotional charge 
            in the tissues,&nbsp;gets erased, too.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Faces look more 
            open, less strained or "scrunched up," and even younger.&nbsp; Eyes 
            get more relaxed.&nbsp; Neck tension is reduced.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The<i> </i>body is 
            literally "reformed" and "cleaned up," and its tissue quality and 
            metabolism is healthier.&nbsp; So it works a lot better physically &amp; 
            is more stress resistant as well.

            </b></font>&nbsp;People find the old stress they had is gone, they don't 
            tighten up in stressful situations as much as they used to, and they 
            let go of their tensing up faster.<font color="#666666"><b><br>

            </b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            <b>This</b></font><b><font color="#666666"> overall openness and 
            "unblocking" has helped many people</font></b>

            <font color="#666666"><b>express themselves more openly and more 
            confidently.&nbsp; And their minds were calmer and clearer.&nbsp;

            </b>

            </font>

            A lot of their old fears due to tension and embedded negative 
            emotions, were now gone.<br>

            <font color="#666666"><b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; My own 
            special multi-faceted program, Postural Integration Plus increases 
            these stress release benefits from the bodywork alone, and adds more 
            personal development.&nbsp; It's especially helpful for trauma 
            release, too, from very old as well as recent experiences.&nbsp;

            </b>

            The energies we absorbed during the past trauma still stay inside 
            the body and therefore keep making our reactions to current stress 
            more than they should be.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><b>&nbsp;<font color="#666666">When 
            we remove the old emotional energies created inside us during past 
            stressful experiences, we no longer react in such a stressful way to 
            our current stressful experiences.&nbsp; </font></b>Netherton and&nbsp; 
            Reichian Therapy techniques add a lot to the releasing we can do 
            with the Bodywork itself.&nbsp; They can actually get out the deeper 
            energies in the organs and remove the negative "belief systems" that 
            say we should get so tensed up in those kinds of situations.</font><font color="#666666"><b><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            </b>

            </font>

            <font face="Arial">People who have already gotten stress and trauma 
            release from deep tissue massage, myofascial release, or other 
            Structural Integration programs including Postural Integration,

            <font color="#666666">find they can use these methods to build on 
            what they've already done.<br>

            <b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
            It has also immediately improved what people have worked on in their 
            psychotherapy and spiritual counseling.&nbsp; As a general rule, 
            whatever we've already worked on mentally and emotionally, gets 
            better when we do the physical and energetic parts, too.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
            Even just Structural Integration itself has helped many people in 
            their ongoing psychotherapy and counseling.<br>

            </a>

            </font>

            <font color="#009933" size="4" face="Arial"><b>My Helpful Bodywork 
            Modifications, enabling...<br>

            My multi-session Travel Program<br>

            <br>

            </b></font>

      <i><b><font face="Arial" color="#FF0000">You can also come to me for a few 
            days' intensive.<br>

      </font></b><font face="Arial" color="#800000"><b><u>My rates</u> for 
            multi-hour intensives are o<u>ften less than the hourly cost</u><br>

      <u>in other areas</u>, including travel costs.&nbsp; Includes free 
            stretching sessions, nutritional advice &amp; optional emotional release 
            processing.<br>

      </b>

      <br>

      </font>

            </i>

            <font face="Arial">

            <font size="1" color="#666666"><br>

            </font>

            <font color="#666666"><b><i>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            </i>In my own Structural Integration approach, I incorporate 
            advanced relengthening techniques in many sessions that usually 
            aren't done in the basic 10-step process. These enable me to get 
            better results, sooner&nbsp; than would be common.<br>

            </b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            <b>I also work in more than one area in each step, also not that 
            common.&nbsp; And I work in longer sessions than the usual hour to 
            hour and fifteen minutes.&nbsp; This all enables me to make people 
            feel better overall, sooner. </b></font>&nbsp;Sometimes, if a person's 
            body is malleable enough, I can relieve even chronic, worsening back 
            pain in a few hours.<font color="#666666"><b><br>

            <font size="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            </font></b><font size="1"><br>

            </font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>&nbsp;I 
            do a lot on the back, shoulders and neck, as well as the head, often 
            right away, and in other sessions as well.</b>&nbsp;<b>This increases 
            flexibility and relaxation even before I begin the usual 
            "unraveling" sequence.&nbsp; It makes that unraveling do more in the 
            first sessions, too.</b>&nbsp; T</font>he repetitive tune ups keep 
            people more relaxed and enable those sessions to do more as well.<font color="#666666"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>Very importantly, this 
            approach increases our "mind-body awareness." </b>&nbsp; <b>Besides 
            being great for athletic performance and stress reduction, people 
            can tell more of what the treatment itself is doing for them.</b>&nbsp;</font> 
            It also helps remove old emotional energies out of the body easier, 
            when they're released from other muscles.<font color="#666666"><br>

            <b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </b></font>

            Doing a lot of the head, neck and back, in the first and&nbsp; many 
            other sessions is not done in the typical week by week 10-step or 
            11-step program prescribed in the basic recipes used by 
            practitioners in other schools. <b><font color="#666666"><br>

            <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; This approach 
            enables me to do "multi-session" travel visits, too.&nbsp; I combine 
            the longer session, do more areas approach, with my unique hands-on 
            method, and the "structural" stretching exercises that help the next 
            Bodywork sessions do more.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; I drive or fly to 
            the person (or group) and stay a few days to a few weeks, or they 
            come to me.&nbsp; With this system, we can do a number of long 
            sessions on consecutive days and make great, fast progress.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font></b>I also 
            include energy work and acupressure, high level nutrition tips, and 
            the optional release techniques,&nbsp;&nbsp; So we can get a lot 
            done right away, in both the purely physical and/or the 
            psycho-somatic realms.<font color="#666666"><br>

            <font size="2"><br>

            <a name="benefits - prof perf program"></a><br>

            </font></font>

            <font color="#009933" size="4"><b>My Whole Person Programs for 
            Professionals</b></font><font color="#666666"><b><br>

            </b><font size="1">

            <br>

            </font>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>

            Just above, I described the benefits received by business 
            professionals and performing artists.&nbsp; So I've put together 
            Performance Enhancement programs, tailored to each personal and 
            professional need.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; My multi-feature 
            approach enables me to help people in more parts of their bodies and 
            minds than with just the Bodywork alone.&nbsp; </b> </font>Many 
            folks say they feel I'm working on a number of levels at once.<font color="#666666"><b>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

            <br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Almost all the features 
            are done right during the Bodywork process itself.&nbsp; So it's a 
            synergistic, whole body and mind approach.&nbsp; Each feature 
            enables the others to do more.</b>&nbsp; </font>I also refer people 
            to features that I, myself don't provide.&nbsp; I'm actually known 
            to be a very knowledgeable resource guide.<br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; These programs, of 
            course, increase physical and professional performance, and 
            simultaneously remove stress, tightness and pain.&nbsp; They also 
            add support, insight and nourishment, in physical, psychological, 
            nutritional and even spiritual ways.<font color="#666666"><br>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b>A key feature in 
            my approach is educating people about their body-minds.&nbsp; It's a 
            show and tell about how humans work, and how we can all make 
            ourselves work better, and more enjoyably.&nbsp; This has worked in 
            both their professional and personal lives.<br>
